EL-DB Transition Guide (Human Readable)

Generated: 2026-04-21 21:49:18

This guide is built from public EL-DB map pages.
It focuses on transitions a person can reason about quickly: exits, teleports, same-map paths, and internal entrances.
Secret paths are intentionally not included by EL-DB and therefore are not represented here.
